As more information is gathered and reviewed, it shapes our understanding of the field, and influences how treatment is rendered. What may have been considered standard of care at one time, is often revealed to be woefully inadequate as more information becomes available. In our profession, we have the unique ability to be able to prevent the vast majority of dental disease, which all of us here at Pier 210 Dental feel strongly is the best, and really only acceptable way to treat our patients. <Text>I have had some serious dental work done starting at an early age due to an accident. As time went on the work done in my childhood needed some work. Dr. Roholt performed a dental implant on my front tooth right before Christmas almost 5 years ago and re-used my temporary crown because I didn't have any insurance and it helped to save my pocket book. With 5 years passing I felt it was time to make the temporary unmatching crown a permanent matching one. I have been very self conscious of my smile since my initial injury but even more self conscious since my teeth didnt match. It prevented me from being me. I loved to smile. I scheduled an appointment with Pier 210 Dental after finding out Dr. Vandewalker was in my network and accepted my insurance. I got my teeth cleaned and expressed to him my insecurities with my teeth and smile. He spent time talking to me about a game plan and told me to go home and think about what we talked about. I did, called the next day to schedule an appointment to get my front tooth fixed. Finally to have teeth that may not all be mine but look like they are was my ultimate dream. Today 12/19/18 I got my new crown. I cried, tears of joy. My smile is back and my teeth (even though not all mine) you would never know! If you are looking for honest dentistry, caring office staff and a great mouth experience Pier 210 Dental is your place. 101066394541077063212< /user_id>
<user_name>Milasdaddy<//user_name>< Time>
1574628010739<//Time>
<Rating>1</Rating>< review>
My wife was in an accident in Irvine, and we live about 33 miles out. So AAA towed the car here as they are a "AAA certified mechanic"  She requested that it  just be repaired enough to be driven, as I do my own work on our cars.
First, they told her that they would not be able to look at her car until after the weekend (this was thursday) eh, okay... sure....
Friday morning they called her and told her that her tie rod end was broken (this I knew) but that her entire steering rack needed to be replaced because it was leaking, and repairs were  going to be $1,900. Now, this is a 2006 camry, car probably isnt worth 1,900 but I digress.
I called a mechanic in my area, asked him how much to replace our steering rack... He said $400 out the door.
So here comes the fun, the wife called and let them know that we were going to come pick up the car... They started to get weird. Wanted to know why, so she told them we got a better quote. They wanted to know how much, so when she said "400" they thought she meant 400 less than their quote... So now, oh guess what.. "well, we could probably go with cheaper parts... and get it down 300-350 less, but just so you know if you take it somewhere else they are probably going to blah blah" Trying everything they could to get her to keep it with them.
First of all, if you could have done it for cheaper, that should have been stated RIGHT AWAY. Not when we decide to take the car somewhere else.
So I get there to pick the car up, and there is no sign of leaking fluid ANYWHERE. Okay, maybe they just put it here? Started the car, still no leaks.
Got the car home, lifted it, and found that it had a broken tie rod as they stated... but absolutely NOTHING wrong with the steering rack. No leaks, no noise...
What was broken, though, was a lower control arm... which they did not mention. I mean, it was clear as day when I got under the car. So I have a feeling they did not even lift the car to actually inspect it. Or, if they did... they missed a major issue which is equally as bad.
So now, they quoted me 1900 to do the steering rack/alignment/tie rod ends.
What the car actually needed: inner tie rod, lower control arm, ball joint.
What I actually paid an honest mechanic: 150 in parts, 150 in labor.
The car is running just as it was before the accident. No issues with the steering rack, no leaking  power steering fluid. And the other mechanic actually pulled the dents out on his own, free of charge.
Please, be careful of predatory mechanics... These guys saw a woman who was desperate to get her car fixed, and jumped on the opportunity to make a quick buck for very little work.
Now, a week later the car is still fine, no leaking power steering fluid, no problems at all with the steering rack. I paid 100 dollars for a diagnosis, and got an incorrect assessment of what was wrong.  And had I not intervened, my wife would have paid the 1900 for 300$ worth of work.<//review>
